< Review>
We had an amazing time on the water with Kayak Trinidad! This was my husband's birthday present, but it was such a treat for me too - I might have loved it even more than he did! It was my first time going solo in an ocean kayak, and I loved how it felt to be steering and powering myself across the water. But my favorite part was definitely the wildlife! We saw harbor seals at eye level, which was a wish come true, and followed the antics of a river otter. The clusters of kelp were so cool to glide over, and I was delighted by the size of the jellyfish we saw! Our guide was terrific and had lots to say about the resident birds and other living things. We paddled around some rocks and bouys and just had a terrific time all morning. I highly recommend Kayak Trinidad: they're a great group of friendly, knowledgeable folks operating out of one of the most beautiful places you'll ever visit.<//Review>

"I Had No Idea..."  That should be the title for this post.  I had no idea of the variety and number of wildlife, marine life, views and experiences we would encounter during a tour of Trinidad Bay.  Pelicans, cormorants,  marbled murrelets, pigeon guillemots, common murres, baby gulls, baby harbor seals, kelp varieties, purple sea urchins, sea stars, sea stacks, sea gardens, rocks, cliffs...  Wow!  Great equipment, professional guide.  Tip:  choose a cool day with overcast for the smoothest seas and paddling.

Update November 2020:  Did a "refresher" lesson - extremely valuable experience and a truly delightful morning on the water.  Added River Otter to the list above, as well!< /text>

Outstanding experience in Humboldt County !
Honestly,  this is the best:  in the company of an experienced, knowledgeable guide, you travel leisurely in another world for 3 hours, exploring the islands in Trinidad Harbor.  You are supplied with all of the safety gear and instruction needed to traverse these icy waters.  You will see seals, all sorts of colorful invertebrates, and, if lucky, whales and dolphins.  You will feel the gentle rise and fall as the kayak floats over the open-ocean swell.  To buy one of these kayaks new is generally over a grandâ€¦so to be able to use one, delivered to the beach, with all of the gear, for 3 hours for a hundred bucks is a ridiculously great deal.  No wonder they are booked up.  This outfit is a treasure of the north coast.</Text>

< Review>
My experience at this clinic was phenomenal. From the wonderful staff who greeted me with joy to Dr. Godinez who is so friendly. I felt right at home. The staffs attention to detail was amazing coupled with the doctors bedside manner put me at ease. I knew I had hearing loss but I just did not want to admit it. I also was terrified hearing aids.

Doctor Godinez I might say has a way with words and he made me feel comfortable with my impairment. He also presented me with all my options and I was amazed that hearing aids were so comfortable and invisible. He fit me with hearing aids and long and behold I could hear again. Lastly after the doctor verified and I confirmed I was happy with my hearing aids. Staff explained the do's and don't. She was so sweet. Even after I was leaving the rest of the staff congratulated me.

I must say they are the Best both Dr. Godinez and staff. They even made me a required appointment in two weeks.< /Review>
